Current Affairs Commentary

Can the United States Change its Silver Policy for China? 14

— End

Since the United States increased the price of silver, China's economic difficulties have multiplied. There is widespread hope that the United States can ease its silver purchasing policy, allowing for a slight respite to alleviate the immediate crisis. In particular, there is fervent anticipation that the U.S. economic mission to China will return home and convey what they have heard and seen to their countrymen, leading to a slight change in past attitudes. However, whether this will be effective remains to be seen. Let us tentatively examine the attitude towards silver prices that the United States has held over the years.

The United States has always been known for its silver production. The silver mining industry has a great influence within the country. Whenever silver prices fall, silver-supporting legislators, concerned with their own interests, always fight tooth and nail. As a result, the United States has used the method of absorbing silver to raise silver prices, not just since today. In 1878, when European countries stopped minting silver coins, silver prices plummeted. The U.S. government immediately passed a bill stipulating that the government would purchase two million to four million dollars worth of silver each month. However, it was still difficult to maintain silver prices. By 1890, a major panic occurred in London and New York. The United States then enacted the Sherman Law, purchasing 4.5 million ounces of raw silver each month at market prices. However, due to increasing silver production, the maintenance strategy ultimately failed. In 1892, silver prices continued to plummet. A monetary conference was convened in Brussels. By 1893, the Sherman Law was declared abolished. Silver prices then rapidly declined from forty-one pence per ounce. Only after the outbreak of the European War did silver prices gradually rebound. On February 10, 1920, silver prices reached their peak. The price of silver in New York rose to one dollar and forty-four cents. The price of silver in London also reached eighty-nine pence. However, in mid-June, silver prices experienced a major reversal, falling by half of the previous increase. Subsequently, silver prices declined sharply. After the devaluation of the British pound in 1931, the price of silver in London fell to twelve pence. The price of American silver also reached its lowest point of twenty-four and a half cents in the following year. The fluctuations in silver prices over these twelve years, like the height of mountains and the depths of valleys, fully demonstrate the ability to change. It is truly a grand spectacle. United States silver legislators, seeking to protect the interests of those they represent, attempted to raise the price of silver to one dollar and twenty-nine cents, making the ratio of gold to silver one to sixteen, thus creating the current situation.

The United States' increase in the price of silver is based on its own interests. Those who seek their own benefit are often driven by greed, not hesitating to harm others to benefit themselves. This is common. If the United States can suddenly change its course, it can only come about in two ways. One is that the supply of silver production increases, becoming overwhelming, ultimately making it difficult to achieve its goal of raising silver prices. The other is that harming others does not benefit oneself, deeply realizing that it does not meet expectations, and resorting to abandonment. In short, unless the Americans themselves want to abandon it and do so, it means they are forced to abandon it.

Silver production is often a byproduct of zinc, lead, and other mines. To increase silver production, it is necessary to increase the main products such as zinc and lead. If zinc and lead become oversupplied as a result, it is questionable whether the gains from higher silver prices can compensate for the losses. Even if that is not the case, silver production will also change due to rising silver prices. At that time, will they raise silver prices again or abandon them? However, this is not what this article wants to discuss. What we want to ask is, do Americans not see raising the price of silver as promoting the purchasing power of silver-using countries? If American trade with China continues to maintain its advantage, then those silver-supporting legislators will be even more vociferous, believing it to be a clever move. To hope that they will change their policy is like asking a tiger for its skin. However, the economic situation in China is the opposite. The higher the price of silver, the more difficult life becomes. Even if American goods are cheap due to the exchange rate, there will eventually be a day when the Chinese are unable to purchase them. That day is not far off. However, China has now reached a point where it relies on others for food and clothing, making it difficult to live without foreign goods. This is painful to say, but it is a fact that cannot be denied. Therefore, in the future, they will inevitably choose the cheapest foreign goods. This is something that American industry and commerce may not be able to compete with. Therefore, while it cannot be said that forcing the Chinese to take this path is the fault of the Americans, it is also due to a misunderstanding of the situation in China and the harm of standing idly by.

Self-help leads to the help of others. Seeking help from others is not as good as seeking help from oneself. Americans have this plan based on their own considerations. We Chinese should also plan from our own perspective and seek new avenues. Knowing that the current economic situation in China involves many issues, with obstacles arising everywhere and riddled with problems, it is not easy to remedy. However, we should not be afraid of difficulties and seek temporary ease, merely begging others for pity. We should brace ourselves, work together, and exhaust our talents and wisdom to resist the external dangers and terrifying waves. Who knows if we will not turn misfortune into good fortune and have a day to celebrate peace and tranquility together?

The Day After the New British Prime Minister Takes Office, He Announces His Policy Direction, Wishing the Whole Country to Unite and Persevere Unwaveringly, So as to Maintain its Leading Position in the World, Foreign Policy Based on the League of Nations 15

(London) Today, new Prime Minister Baldwin announced to the nation via broadcast that a government of national unity should continue to exist to ensure the continuation of trust and the maintenance of commercial revival. The new government intends to strive for peace and disarmament, believing that there will eventually be a day of success. He intends to adopt new procedures, with two cabinet members handling foreign affairs, so that the government can pay special attention to the affairs of its League of Nations membership. He also stated that Britain's foreign policy is based on its League of Nations membership, which should be clearly pointed out. Mr. Baldwin then reiterated the main points of his speech in Worcestershire. He concluded, "I wish the spirit of unity to continue unwaveringly, so that our country can consolidate and maintain its leading position in the trend towards world prosperity, world freedom, world peace, and progress." (Reuters, 8th)

(London) Today, new Prime Minister Baldwin, in his first speech in Worcestershire after taking office, stated the current situation at home and abroad, saying that our responsibility to safeguard democracy and orderly freedom is greater than that of any country in the world today. He praised the achievements of the former Prime Minister. He went on to praise the achievements of former Prime Minister MacDonald during his tenure. He had worked with MacDonald for several years, and they would continue to have close relations. He dared to say that a partisan government could never have achieved what a government of national unity had achieved in the past four years. (Reuters, 8th)

Simultaneous Consideration of National Defense and Security

Mr. Baldwin then mentioned the issue of national defense and collective security systems, saying that the current situation in Europe is precarious, which you all know well and need not be elaborated. However, the government's duty is to state frankly that Britain's defense equipment cannot be perfected until international arms limitations are implemented. On the one hand, we must defend our country, and on the other hand, we must promote a collective security system. However, if our own strength is insufficient, advocating a collective security system will not have a corresponding effect. We are fighting for arms limitations in Geneva, and at the same time, we are not neglecting our own security. The reason is this: In short, the purpose of our British policy is to seek peace for other countries and for our own people, and to seek security for our own people and for the people of Europe. (Havas, 8th)

Democracy is Better Than Dictatorship

He then elaborated on the political positions of major countries such as Italy, Russia, Germany, the United States, and France, saying that the great democratic countries that can enjoy the blessings of security are Britain (cheers). He then discussed the dictatorship system, saying that this system begins and ends with the period during which the dictator himself can maintain his power. The characteristic of the dictatorship system is the possibility of rapid and unexpected actions, which is often absent in democratic countries that adhere to the principles of a democratic constitution.

German Sky Armaments

He then mentioned Germany's sky armaments, saying that this move had been kept secret for a long time, but it was completed with two years of work.

Anxiety Over the Italian-Abyssinian Case

He then mentioned the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, saying that all countries in Europe are now uneasy about this. We are now suddenly encountering this kind of difficulty and possible danger. This matter makes it even more necessary for governments around the world to maintain their security and strength.

Strengthening Diplomatic Power

He then said that he had made changes to the administrative aspects of the Foreign Office to make it easier for Foreign Office personnel to handle affairs and to cooperate with the League of Nations more easily.

Progress in Domestic Industry

Finally, he mentioned the current situation in the country, saying that industrial recovery is progressing well. We still need cheap currency to benefit industry and reduce the cost of living. We are now enjoying the benefits of both. The unemployment problem is also showing signs of turning for the better. Old-line Conservative Party members are now worried that they will lose their party's prestige under the current government, but there is no need to worry. The National Liberal Party and the Labour Party have both given assurances that in the next presidential election, they intend to help Conservative Party members who are preparing to run for election to maintain their positions. (Reuters, 8th)

British Government Economic Advisor Will Be Sent to China This Autumn to Investigate China's Financial and Economic Situation 16

(London) Today, the Foreign Office announced that Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the British government's chief economic advisor, will depart for China in August. This statement is sufficient to indicate the British government's attention to China's recent financial and economic developments. The Soviet-Czech Mutual Assistance Treaty Was Signed in Moscow Yesterday 20

Further Concluding a Cultural Agreement, the Two Slavic Nations Join Hands

(Moscow) The Soviet-Czech mutual assistance treaty was signed today by Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov and Czech Foreign Minister Beneš. The Czech Foreign Minister is currently on a return visit to Moscow. An important clause in the treaty stipulates that the treaty will only take effect when the invaded country receives assistance from France. Other than that, the treaty is roughly the same as the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance treaty. The first three clauses are identical. (Reuters, 9th).

(Moscow) Czech Foreign Minister Beneš arrived here this morning and met with People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov at 3 p.m., beginning talks that lasted until 5 p.m. The discussion concerned the signing of a cultural agreement between the Soviet Union and Czechoslovakia. According to this agreement, the two sides will be able to hold art exhibitions and translate literary works, and establish procedures to protect copyrights. Litvinov held a banquet in the evening to welcome Beneš and gave a speech praising him, calling him "one of the most distinguished figures in the Czech and Slovak free movement, one of the founding fathers of Czechoslovakia, and one of the most forceful advocates of international cooperation to maintain peace. The recent conclusion of a mutual assistance treaty between the Soviet Union and Czechoslovakia is sufficient to confirm and consolidate the mutual friendship and the shared view of the two sides on appeasing Europe." He also said that while a certain country is now doing its best to oppose the collective security system, we must also do our best to uphold this system. "The friendship between the Soviet Union and Czechoslovakia has always been based on a spirit of mutual understanding and close cooperation. In the future, the development of economic and cultural relations between the two sides should still be guided by this spirit." Beneš replied in Russian that there was no difference in views between the two sides and that their common policy was a policy of maintaining peace. "My trip is also a prelude to increasingly close cooperation in this common policy," he said. Beneš is scheduled to visit the Moscow Kremlin district at 9:30 a.m. tomorrow and meet with Kalinin, Chairman of the Central Executive Committee, and Molotov, Chairman of the People's Committee. General Secretary of the Central Committee Stalin will also participate. (Havas, 8th)

(Moscow) Soviet newspapers welcomed the arrival of Czechoslovak Foreign Minister Beneš in Moscow and published his biography and photographs. Radek, in the Soviet Government Gazette, announced Beneš's outstanding position among the great bourgeois diplomats of post-war Europe. He continued, "Czechoslovakia is a post-war country that has played an important role in Central Europe, exceeding our expectations. German imperialism, under the fascist banner, demands to move south, threatening Czechoslovakia. The outposts of German fascism have been established within Czech territory and are joining hands with the enemies of independent Czechoslovakia. The Czech Republic is now facing a serious problem, namely, fighting to maintain its own survival. Beneš has played a leading role in seeing the good of the Soviet Union, and has made efforts to promote friendly relations between other countries and the Soviet Union. Therefore, Soviet citizens will warmly welcome him, because they know how to hate their enemies and respect their friends. The Soviet Union is not pursuing any aggression. It is only striving to maintain peace. It is sincerely pleased that it can be so friendly with the Czech Republic." (TASS, 8th)

Completing an Important Mission, General Göring Returns to His Country, Visits Hitler to Report on His Eastern Journey 21

German Monks' City: Minister of Aviation General Göring and his wife returned from the Yugoslav capital and arrived here at 5:30 p.m. Mr. Göring immediately went to Berchtesgaden near this city to visit Führer Hitler to report on his travels to Hungary, Bulgaria, and Yugoslavia. (Havas, 8th)

Pan-Germanic Slogans Can Be Seen Everywhere

Germany is not just the German Empire. All places that speak German and have German ideas should belong to German territory. Therefore, Merano and Memel should both be German cities." The "Oriental Clipper" Conducts Blind Flight Tests, Especially Using Wireless Radio as a Compass 23

Alameda, USA: The "Oriental Clipper" large aircraft, which will soon fly between San Francisco and Guangzhou, today conducted a "blind" landing test here. It will probably depart for Honolulu and Midway next Wednesday or Thursday. Today's "blind" landing meant that even eyewitnesses could not see that all the personnel in the aircraft could not see outside, because after the aircraft took off, the curtains were pulled down, completely isolating it from the outside world, except for a low-ranking person who could see outside. At this time, the aircraft flew out to sea for 150 miles, then turned back and landed at the original location. All driving targets relied entirely on wireless radio as a compass. The low-ranking lookout personnel were only for precautionary purposes and provided no assistance. It is reported that this test has shown that wireless guidance of aircraft is completely successful. (National News Agency, 8th)

Sapporo: A gas explosion occurred at 1:30 a.m. today in the 3rd pit of the Asano Mine in Numata, Uryu County, Hokkaido. U.S. Senate Silver Faction Members Launch Campaign to Raise Silver Prices, Meeting Scheduled for Today 31

Demand Increase to $1.29 Per Ounce and Request Treasury Secretary Explain the Reason for Silver Price Decline

(Washington) Democratic Senator McCarran has convened a meeting of Senate silver faction members today, Monday, to discuss methods of raising the price of silver to $1.29 per ounce. McCarran stated that the British are currently exerting efforts in various countries to promote opposition to the American silver purchasing policy. He has therefore sent a letter to Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, questioning whether the Treasury Department has directly or indirectly sold silver bullion from the Federal Stabilization Fund, and if so, the total amount and price. McCarran also requested the Treasury Secretary to explain the reason for the recent decline in silver prices and asked what methods the Treasury Department is currently employing to implement the congressional silver purchasing mandate. A passage in McCarran's letter reads, "There are widespread rumors in the world market that the United States will abandon its silver purchasing policy. This type of rumor is unfounded, and I firmly believe that you can inform the nation that the government is still earnestly implementing the silver purchasing law." (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Washington) Nevada Democratic Senator McCarran has convened a meeting of the silver bloc, hoping to relaunch a campaign to force silver prices to rise to $1.29 per ounce and to quell rumors that the Treasury Department intends to change its silver policy. The senator sent a lengthy letter to Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, requesting an explanation for the recent decline in silver prices and inquiring about the origins of rumors concerning the Treasury Department's actions. The timing of the silver bloc meeting has not yet been determined, but it is expected to take place within the next week if the Treasury Secretary responds to the letter. Meanwhile, Colorado Democratic Senator Adams and others believe that there is no need to relaunch a campaign to promote further silver purchases, and that the silver policy is progressing satisfactorily. New York news: Many brokers there believe that once Mexico releases its newly minted silver coins into the market, the trend of silver prices rising towards $1.29 per ounce may resume. They also stated that when Mexico encountered difficulties, the United States suddenly stopped raising silver prices, but Mexico urgently desires the rise in prices and only seeks temporary relief. Once Mexico circulates its new silver coins, it can sit back and watch silver prices rise steadily. Mexican authorities have apparently learned from well-informed sources that they must protect their minted coins, preventing silver prices from rising to at least $1.29 per ounce. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

U.S. Gold Reserves Reach Unprecedented Record of 89 Billion Yuan 32

Central Government Spending Averaging 20 Million Yuan Daily

(Washington) The Department of Commerce announced today that the national treasury's gold reserves have reached an unprecedented record of $8,891,648,029, of which $52,180,425 was shipped from France last week. The Treasury Department released figures showing that from March 4, 1914, to June 5 of this year, the total expenditure of the central government was $15,393,000,000, exceeding the normal amount by approximately one-fold. During the same period, revenue was $7,303,000,000, resulting in a deficit of approximately 80 billion yuan. The current total national debt is $28,783,000,000, which is $20 billion more than the total cost of the European War. Since President Roosevelt took office, the average daily expenditure of various departments and agencies of the central government has been 20 million yuan. (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Peace in Gran Chaco Looks Promising, Ceasefire Agreement Reached 33

Stipulation for Immediate Cessation of Hostilities and Submission of Disputes to Arbitration, Bolivian and Paraguayan Representatives Have Verbally Indicated Acceptance

Capital of Argentina: Regarding the dispute over the Gran Chaco territory between Bolivia and Paraguay, Argentina, Chile, the United States, Peru, and Brazil acted as mediators, inviting the foreign ministers of Bolivia and Paraguay to hold a meeting here. A final agreement has been reached regarding the mediation method, stipulating that the two countries immediately cease hostilities and submit the dispute to arbitration. The foreign ministers of both Bolivia and Paraguay have verbally indicated acceptance of this agreement, which will be signed after ratification by the presidents of their respective countries. The draft agreement was jointly drafted by the Peruvian Ambassador to Argentina, Barreda Las, and the Director of Political Affairs of the Argentine Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Coste. The draft was initially signed by the Argentine Minister of Finance, Lamas. Lamas declared, "I am honored to have participated in drafting the agreement. I believe the Bolivian-Paraguayan War will end from this point onward, and I hope this will be the last war on the American continent." (Havas dispatch, 9th)

Madrid: Most of the land in Spain is owned by former nobles. Their land holdings account for 577,000 hectares of the country. For the purpose of resolving the land issue, the government has established a Land Reform Institute, whose task is to collect land and distribute it to farmers for resettlement. More than 13,000 farming families have already benefited, and the process is still underway. To date, approximately 100,000 hectares of land have been reformed, of which 88,000 hectares belong to large landowners. "Debate Newspaper" has heavily criticized this reform. Several experts from the institute have filed lawsuits in court. Former Minister of Agriculture Benayas is one of the experts. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

The Question of Greece's Form of Government, Republic or Monarchy, Determined by Referendum 35

Athens: The National Assembly election is scheduled for tomorrow. The election date was originally set for May 19, then postponed to June 2, and finally delayed by another week to allow all opposition parties to participate in the election. The government faction, led by Prime Minister Tsaldaris, and the faction led by Deputy Prime Minister and Army Minister General Kondylis, do not wish to raise the issue of changing the form of government to the National Assembly, and intend to hold a separate referendum to decide the matter. Conversely, the royalist party led by former Minister without Portfolio Metaxas advocates declaring a restoration without waiting for a referendum. Therefore, whether Greece will continue to use the republican system or change to a monarchy will be discernible from the results of tomorrow's election. According to "Anexartitos" newspaper, Minister without Portfolio Mavromichalis went to Paris on Wednesday to meet with the deposed King George, to explain the government's views on the propaganda campaign of Metaxas' party and its possible impact. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

Athens: The National Assembly election was held today. Athens, Piraeus, and the provinces began voting in succession from early morning. Although the streets were extremely crowded, no incidents were reported. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

Vatican City: Today, reliable sources here disclosed that Pope Pius IX is currently studying ways to improve the method of electing the Pope. The purpose of this reform is to unify the Catholic Church and the Eastern Church. It is said that the Pope has summoned experts from various denominations to express their opinions on how to enable the Eastern Church to directly participate in the election through its representatives. Therefore, bishops of the Eastern Church may also attend future episcopal conferences. Nanjing-Shanghai and Jiangnan Railways Changed to Connect Outside the City 38

(Nanjing) Regarding the project to connect the Nanjing-Shanghai and Jiangnan Railways, the Ministry of Interior submitted a proposal to requisition private land inside the city. The company later realized that connecting inside the city, although it could utilize the Nanjing City Small Railway, would require building bridges over the Qinhuai River and the moat, which would be very costly. It was decided to abandon the original plan and connect outside the city instead. The line will run northwest from the Yuhua Road terminal, along the foot of Yuhua Terrace Mountain to Honghuadi outside Tongji Gate, for the Jiangnan Railway. Then, from the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway Bureau, a branch line will connect directly to Honghuadi near Yaohuamen. A transfer station will be set up in Honghuadi. The two railway bureaus are currently discussing this plan. The announced land requisition law for the city will be revoked after the route outside the city is determined. It is reported that funding has been secured for the lack of track construction costs for the Nanjing-Wuhu section. The Ministry of Railways and the Construction Committee guaranteed the issuance of 3 million company bonds for principal repayment. The company recently needed funds and paid 800,000 yuan in bond subscriptions in advance, pledging 600,000 yuan to the Shanghai Bank, which was also guaranteed by the Construction Committee and paid out immediately. (Special dispatch, 9th)

Netherlands East Indies Government Prohibits Chinese Schools from Registering with China 72

While claiming not to interfere with Chinese schools registering with the Chinese government, they have issued a deadline for already registered schools to cancel their registration within three months.

Surabaya Correspondence: In mid-May, more than ten representatives of Chinese schools in Surabaya were summoned to the Political Department of the Police Department. They were received by Mr. de Vries, who first recorded the names of the attendees and the names of the schools they represented. He then asked the school representatives whether they had registered with the Chinese central government. Everyone replied that they had not. Mr. de Vries then announced the attitude of the Netherlands East Indies government on this matter. It was stated that because the Chinese government has regulations for registration matters, requiring that registered schools must teach Party principles and that their teachers must be members of the Party, and because the Kuomintang is a political organization while schools here are not allowed to be infiltrated by political elements, this point is considered to be conflicting. The government here does not refuse registration with the Chinese government for schools here, but any teachers who teach politics must be dismissed from their teaching positions and may be deported if necessary. Therefore, those who have already registered must cancel the original case with the Chinese registration authority within three months and submit evidence of the cancellation to the Political Department. Furthermore, while those present acknowledge that they have not registered with the Chinese government, if this is found to be the case in the future, all their rights may be forfeited. At that point, each attendee signed a document, and the meeting was adjourned.

An Account of an Inspection in the Northwest 73

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya

Scenery along the Pinghan Railway and General Conditions in Ding County

To observe the work of the Chinese National Association of the Mass Education Movement in Ding County, Hebei, I transferred from Zhengzhou to the Pinghan Railway and boarded the evening express train northward. The train, coming from Hankou, originally had many empty seats, but when a university tour group boarded at Zhengzhou, it suddenly became crowded. The nimble male students were the first to board, invariably occupying two or three seats each, vying to offer seats to the female students. Some were busy elsewhere, trying to manage this or that, and for a time the sounds of laughter and singing almost completely drowned out the clatter of the wheels on the rails.

The train arrived at the Yellow River South Station and stopped to repair the locomotive. It started moving again after a long while, then passed through a tunnel about two li long. Immediately after exiting the tunnel was the Yellow River Railway Bridge. The train slowly crossed the bridge, and looking down, one could see the turbid waves surging into the sky, flowing eastward. The bridge is about six li long and originally had 103 arches, three of which were destroyed during the war. These were repaired by dismantling three arches from the side, so there are now exactly 100 arches. The insurance period has long expired. In the past, it took six or seven minutes to cross the bridge, but now it takes more than twenty minutes to avoid violent shaking and the danger of overturning. The bridge piers are about 15 meters deep, and in recent years the bridge foundations have been repeatedly eroded by floods. Especially during the great flood of 1931, the roots of the piers were almost exposed. The Railway Bureau urgently dumped large quantities of stones under each bridge pier to resist the force of the water. However, since so many stones were dumped, they formed a dam, and it was feared that the riverbed upstream would rise and cause flooding. Therefore, the Henan Provincial Government notified the Railway Bureau not to dump any more stones into the river. As for the funds for rebuilding the new bridge, the Railway Bureau had long been setting aside "depreciation fees" from its operating income on an annual basis, which had accumulated into a large sum. Construction should have started long ago, but unfortunately it was seized during the Zhili-Fengtian War, and again during the 1930 campaign. The designated funds have disappeared. Currently, only a foreign supervisor is hired to inspect the bridge once a month to verify whether it is safe for traffic, which is said to be very risky. Recently, the Ministry of Railways, together with the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, has surveyed the area slightly to the east of the original bridge to build a new bridge. The estimated cost is about twenty to thirty million yuan, and there are rumors of borrowing from the Economic Commission and the Boxer Indemnity Fund Committee.

Around three or four o'clock in the clear morning, the sky gradually brightened, and the train had already left Henan and entered Hebei. It passed Wanghuabao, north of Handan County, known locally as Huangliangmeng, where there is a Han Ancestral Temple. Someone recounted the local mythology, which was vivid and moving. Later, the train arrived at Xingtai (the old Shuncheng Prefecture seat, also the Julu where Zhang Zhou raised an army at the end of the Han Dynasty). There were tall smokestacks and electrical factories, and industry and commerce were relatively developed. Many people got on and off the train. Matouzhen burns coke in brick-built, open-air circular kilns arranged neatly in rows, like dozens of large vats buried underground. The fierce flames roared, and the heat was unbearable for even a moment. Shijiazhuang has many new-style buildings with red tiles and green bricks, tall buildings, and weeping willows, creating a pleasant scene. The area is where the Zhengtai Railway connects with the Pinghan Railway, and most of the goods entering and exiting Shanxi pass through here, so it is becoming increasingly prosperous. From here to Zhengding, Xinle, and all the way to the destination of Ding County, the fertile fields became increasingly vast. The distant mountains were verdant, and the new leaves on the wild trees were a beautiful sight all along the way.

Ding County is about sixty li wide from east to west and about ninety li long from north to south, with an area of ​​5,400 square li. There are more than 68,000 households and an estimated total population of about 400,000. The area is flat and without mountains, a plain with sandy soil. In terms of fertility, it is not the best. About 70% to 80% of all farmland relies on well water for irrigation, and dozens of hectares of rice paddies rely on ditch and river irrigation. According to a survey by the Mass Education Association, self-cultivating farmers account for 63%, self-cultivating and renting land account for 24%, self-cultivating and renting out land account for 5%, pure tenant farmers account for 5%, and others account for 3%. There are a total of more than 1.5 million mu of farmland. Households with less than 25 mu of land account for 63%, households with 25 to 49 mu account for 23%, households with 50 to 99 mu account for 6%, and households with more than 100 mu account for only 1%.

The main agricultural products are millet and wheat, followed by beans, sorghum, cotton, sweet potatoes, corn, peanuts, barley, and others. The production of cotton and peanuts has tended to increase in recent years. Industrial products include homespun cloth, reed mats, willow baskets, reed screens, zhaoli sieves, and other items. The main export goods are cotton, wheat, sesame, peanuts, Yali pears (Snowflake pears), dates, grapes, pigs, chicken eggs, Zhuang cloth, willow baskets, sesame oil, peanut oil, and eye medicine (known as Dingzhou eye medicine), with a total annual value of more than 3 million yuan. The major import goods are millet, foreign flour, sorghum, black beans, rice, coal, kerosene, matches, cigarettes, salt, porcelain, foreign cloth, foreign thread, paint, bicycles, medicines, decorations, and so on, with an annual value of more than 2.9 million yuan. Domestic goods account for about 2.4 million yuan, and the rest are foreign goods.

In terms of rural economy, there are about 68,000 farm households in the county. The total annual tax burden is more than 400,000 yuan. Farm households with debt account for 67% of the total, about 46,000 households. Among the farm households that borrow money, those with less than 20 mu of land account for 63%, those with 20 to 24 mu account for 24%, and those with more than 40 mu account for only 13%. The interest rate on loans is usually 2.5%, and sometimes as high as 5%. Cases of families having their entire property confiscated due to accumulated debt are heard of every year. There are about 2,000 beggars.

In terms of school education, there is the Provincial No. 9 Middle School, the County Normal School, the County Women's Normal School (the vocational school was closed last year), the attached elementary school of the Men's Normal School, the attached middle and elementary schools of the Women's Normal School, 21 township-run male higher elementary schools, 2 female higher elementary schools, 322 male primary schools, and 96 female primary schools. There are no less than several hundred mass schools and people's schools. Sixty-two percent of young people are illiterate, and 60% of school-age children are not in school. Among the 400,000 people in the county, 6,000 have graduated from higher elementary school, about 1,800 have graduated from junior high school, and 460 have graduated from university. In terms of health, there are about 450 doctors in the county, an average of one per village, and more than 400 pharmacies. Common diseases include eye, intestinal, stomach, sore, tuberculosis, infantile convulsions, throat, rash, and skin diseases. In recent years, the number of people addicted to white flour has been increasing, and it is being strictly prohibited. In terms of religion, there are about 7,000 Muslims, about 6,000 Catholics, and about 500 Christians. The general public worships idols, and those with secondary or higher education mostly do not believe in gods. There are about 1,000 temples in total. In terms of customs, early marriage is common. Men often marry before the age of sixteen, and women often marry before the age of eighteen. Most wives are older than their husbands. Girls under the age of sixteen no longer bind their feet. The people are more knowledgeable than in neighboring counties.

According to the conclusion of the survey by the Mass Education Association, it is believed that the county can represent the state of rural society in North China. The four major ills of ignorance, poverty, weakness, and selfishness are obvious. The majority of the people are still illiterate, have insufficient nutrition, are in a state of illness and weakness, and lack a public spirit. It is necessary to find ways to cultivate the people's intelligence, productivity, strength, solidarity, otherwise there is no foundation for rural construction. Therefore, in recent years, the Association's experimental work in Ding County has revealed four major areas of education and three major approaches, which is truly a prescription for the right disease.

The Situation in North China is Easing; Shang Zhen Takes Office in Tianjin and Discusses Troop Transfers and Stationing 74

Beiping Dispatch. Thanks to the authorities' effective maintenance of public order, the public in Beiping and Tianjin is still calm, which is not as intense as rumors would suggest. The Hebei Provincial Government first moved from Tianjin to Baoding, and the entire move was completed today. The Hebei Provincial Party Department has also decided to move to Baoding. The files and documents of each department will be boxed up starting today (8th). The Pinghan Railway Bureau has agreed to allocate vehicles, and the first batch of files can be shipped tonight. The members of the Provincial Party Department have already set off yesterday. Staff members such as secretaries can all report to work in Baoding within three days. The Beiping Municipal Party Department is operating as usual.

Shang Zhen, the newly appointed garrison commander of Tianjin and acting mayor, delayed taking office after the central government announced his appointment, pending the promulgation of the organizational regulations for the garrison command by the central government, negotiating the command's expenses, and transferring garrison troops. After repeated urgings from all parties, Tianjin Mayor Zhang Ting'e sent his representative Liu Junming to Beiping to urge him to take office quickly. Shang said that the organizational regulations for the garrison command had been promulgated in Beiping, and all matters in Beiping had been prepared. This morning (8th) at about 7 o'clock, he received Liu Rongming at his private residence on Nanchang Street, and at about 9 o'clock, he went to Jurentang to meet with He Yingqin, the acting chairman of the Military Sub-Committee, to ask for instructions on taking office. He then dispatched his staff officer Guo Renfu, Fan Zheyuan, and guard captain Li Shaobai to lead a detachment of more than 50 adjutants and guards to Tianjin by train on the Beining Railway. In the afternoon at 3 o'clock, Shang Zhen and Liu Yunfang, the secretary-general of the 32nd Army, went to the East Station of Qianmen and boarded the train to Tianjin. Among those who came to the station to see him off were Bao Yulin, He Qigong, Wang Zhuoran, and Fu Zhang, more than 20 people. Before leaving, he issued the following statement to reporters. The security of Tianjin is a very important matter. I originally intended to take up the post of acting mayor and the post of garrison commander at the same time after arriving in Tianjin. However, due to time constraints, I will first go to the municipal government to consult with Mayor Zhang (Ting'e) and then take up the post of garrison commander. The garrison command will also be established at the same time. The 51st Army will be transferred, and the defense forces in Tanggu, Dagu, Yangliuqing, and Machang will be replaced by the 32nd Army. The two divisions of the army in Luzon have been designated to arrive by land within two days. The army headquarters will remain temporarily in Beiping, and Chief of Staff Fu Liping will remain in Beiping to preside over all matters. The Tianjin police are sufficient to maintain public order, and there is no need to station troops in the city. After I have completed all the arrangements in Tianjin, I will return to Beiping to visit Chairman He.

According to sources, Shang Zhen's old friend Wang Yitang went to Tianjin last night (7th) to liaise with all parties on behalf of Shang Zhen, along with Cao Rulin, a retired official in Tianjin. The results were smooth, so Shang Zhen went to Tianjin today and will report to the municipal government tomorrow without holding any ceremony. The date of the establishment of the garrison command will be determined after Shang Zhen arrives in Tianjin. The internal organization has been completely decided in Beiping. Chen Zikuan has been appointed as the chief of the military affairs department.

The Japanese military attaché to the Embassy, ​​Isoya Renjie, arrived in Tianjin from Shanghai the day before yesterday to convene a meeting of senior officers of the Japanese army stationed in Tianjin to discuss their views on the Hebei issue. Today, he and Sakai, the chief of staff of the Tianjin Garrison Headquarters, arrived in Beiping by train on the Beining Railway at 6:40 pm. After getting off the train, they went to the Fusang Hotel to stay and are scheduled to visit He Yingqin tonight to discuss the Hebei issue.

The Annihilation of the Red Bandits in Fujian and Jiangxi is Imminent; Peng Hu, a Fake Central Committee Member, Details the Reasons for the Failure 75

Fuzhou Dispatch. Five hundred-plus people from the 19th Regiment and one part of the 12th Regiment of the Fake Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region were completely captured in Xianyou a month ago. Peng Hu, the Fake Political Commissar, submitted a detailed statement on the organization and reasons for the failure of the Fujian-Jiangxi Red Bandits while being held in the Fourth District Administrative Commissioner's Office. The details are as follows:

The Internal Situation of the Fake Organization

The original organization and armed situation in Fujian and Jiangxi, the Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region was originally directly under the command of the Fake Military Commission. After the National Army moved into Changting and Ruijin, a Central District was established in Ruijin, with Xiang Ying as the Fake Central District Commander and Political Commissar, and He Chang as the Fake Central District Political Department Director, governing six districts including Southern Jiangxi, Zhejiang and Fujian, Northern Fujian, and Western Fujian. Therefore, Fujian and Jiangxi were also under the jurisdiction of the Fake Central Government. The organization under the Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region includes the Headquarters, Political Department, Supply Department, and Health Department. The commander is the current surrendered Regiment Commander Song Yuanquan, the Political Commissar is Zhong Xunren, the Political Director is Peng Hu, the Supply Department Director is Xie Wu, the Health Department Director is He Chenke, and the Chief of Staff is Xu Jianghan. Under the Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region, there are three sub-districts. The first sub-district was originally in Guihua. After the 52nd Division of the National Army moved into Guihua, the first sub-district was abolished. The commander was Qiu Shangcong, and the Political Commissar was Wen Hanzhen. The second sub-district was in Anyuan. The commander was Wang Youcheng, who died in battle with the National Army in the Shicheng area. The Political Commissar was Xiao Mingxing. The third sub-district was in Hengjiang. The commander is unknown, and the Political Commissar was Liu Banghua.

Inability to Fight the Political Line

Regarding the political line, after the National Army achieved successive victories and the Communist bandits were increasingly annihilated, the Fake Central Government changed its line. This was instructed in December of last year. In February of this year, after the Fake Central District was wiped out, wireless communication was lost, and instructions could not be given. There was no contact with any party. Therefore, the current line is unknown. The Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region is currently implementing the line according to the previous instructions of the Fake Central District.

Guerrilla Tactics Failed to Achieve Results

The main point of this surrender is that the implementation of the political line instructed by the Fake Central District is fundamentally unworkable and counterproductive. Not only has it failed to maintain its own strength, but the number of personnel has decreased daily, halving in just three months. The independent teams are no different. The neighboring fake military regions, such as Southern Jiangxi and Zhejiang and Fujian, have been wiped out. In terms of replenishment, there is no source. The flexible guerrilla tactics were constantly surrounded and attacked by the army. For example, Minxi was defeated by the 52nd and 75th Divisions in Tangdi, Shaxi, and Yuanxi. This is because the people have all awakened, and no one reports any news. Everywhere is like being blind. From this point of view, the so-called nationwide counter-offensive is even more delusional and deceptive. (1) Material difficulties, with no source of origin. We brought only 10,000 yuan from the original treasury, and each person was given one jiao for food every day. It is now used up. Clothes and shoes have not been replenished. Sometimes there is no food for three or four days. (2) Reduced personnel, casualties in combat, and a large number of sick transfers. Not to mention fighting, even daily marching will be exhausted. Moreover, there is no source of supplies. (3) The people have awakened. Every time we arrive at a place, no man, woman, or child guides us. No one walks, and we cannot pass. We march only 20 li per day. In some places, the people use force to deal with us.

Seeking Survival Only Through Surrender

Based on the above-mentioned practical difficulties, annihilation is imminent. To implement communism is even more delusional. After repeated deliberation, we have realized our mistakes and are determined to turn over a new leaf and work for the Party and the country and for the benefit of the people on the road to the Three People's Principles. This time we could have all surrendered together, but Zhong Xunren, a Fake Central Committee member, Chen Changqing, the director of the Provincial Suppression Committee, and Yang Daoming, the chairman of the Provincial Government, opposed it and insisted on not coming. Therefore, we only brought a battalion. More will come later. The troops that came this time are the Fake 19th Regiment and two companies of the 12th Regiment, plus a direct company and a guard team, forming two battalions with more than 700 people and more than 400 guns. The military region has long been abolished. The troops remaining in Fujian and Jiangxi have no unified command. (June 8th)

Anhui Province Continues Work Relief 76

The Investigation and Relief Office has moved from Anqing to Wuhu; first, the construction of the branch road from Wuxikou to Jiuhuashan

Wuhu Dispatch. The Anhui Investigation and Relief Office of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Famine Relief in Various Provinces has been handling relief work in disaster areas since last winter, under the direction of the Venerable Hongsan. The winter and emergency relief have come to an end, but the severely affected areas are still in dire need of relief. Hongsan and the Shanghai General Association have agreed to allocate another 40,000 yuan for additional investigation and relief. To facilitate distribution, the Investigation and Relief Office has been moved from Anqing to Wuhu in recent days and has begun operations. The provincial government has issued orders to military and police agencies to assist in protection. However, according to on-the-ground investigations, the losses from the bandit and drought disasters in Anhui Province last year totaled 49 counties, with more than 8.7 million disaster victims, most of whom could not survive without relief. The tragedy of the disaster is beyond the imagination of those who have not experienced it firsthand. Therefore, it is believed that it is necessary to expand relief. Together with the Anhui Provincial Government Disaster Area Fundraising Committee and other agencies, comprehensive relief will be provided first. This is slightly different from the purpose of charity relief, which is to relieve the dead rather than the poor, but it is necessary to do so for the sake of the actual disaster situation. Personnel have been dispatched to the severely affected counties to conduct investigations and relief. After the relief funds were distributed, there were still twelve counties that had not benefited. Repeated requests were made to the General Association, and another 60,000 yuan was re-issued to carry out work relief. The counties are those that did not receive sufficient allocations from the previous emergency winter relief. The General Association has designated Xuancheng, Luan, Quanjiao, Chuxian, Jiaoan, Tianchang, Xuyi, Jiashan, and other eight counties. The amount of allocation has been determined. Regarding the implementation plan for work relief, the Anhui Construction Department has been contacted once. The principles stipulated are to construct water conservancy projects in the eight counties. The work relief funds total 60,000 yuan, of which 25,000 yuan were originally for purchasing seeds, but since the planting season has passed, they have also been transferred to work relief. The first step is to build the branch road from Wuxikou to Jiuhuashan on the Gutun Road, which is about 13 kilometers long. Jiuhuashan is a famous scenic area in the province, and about 300,000 to 400,000 people visit and burn incense there every year. The construction of this road will make transportation more convenient. The Anhui Construction Department has sent Section Chief Qi Qun to Wuhu to discuss this matter. As for the work relief in other counties, personnel will be sent to the counties to inspect and start work separately according to local needs and the situation of the disaster victims after consulting with the General Association in Shanghai. (5th)

Songjiang: Gao Disheng's Home in Zhangze is Robbed 77

At about 1 am on the 5th, the home of Gao Disheng in Zhangze Fifteen Township was suddenly robbed by a dozen or so bandits armed with wooden sticks and three muzzle-loading guns. They searched wildly, injuring the owner and his two sons, Shuizhang and Yonglou. After the robbery, they fled towards the Jinshan County boundary in a chaotic clamor. It is reported that the loss of gold jewelry and beads amounted to as much as six or seven hundred yuan. The Public Security Bureau has been requested to order an arrest.

Haimen: Workers at the Third Factory Suddenly Strike 78

The Dasheng Third Factory in Changlezhen, Third District, experienced a strike on the 18th of last month due to layoffs and wage cuts. After officials from the Party and government agencies went to persuade them, work safely resumed on the 27th. However, yesterday (the 7th) at 6 pm, during the shift change between the day and night workers, a strike suddenly broke out. After the day workers left the factory, they remained gathered and refused to disperse. The night workers also stopped outside the factory and delayed entering. At the time, the noise was loud, the order was chaotic, and the situation was unusually heavy. Yuan Zhongqi, the chief of the labor department of the factory, came to the county to report the strike to the Party and government agencies. After receiving the report, the county government immediately dispatched more than 20 members of the security team in three cars to maintain order, and Xiao Shuen, a standing member of the county Party department, and Hu Yirong, the secretary of the county government, went to investigate the truth of the strike to determine how to handle it.

Wuxi: Deadline for Collecting Second Phase Opium Licenses 79

The county's Opium Prohibition Committee has already set a deadline for opium smokers to exchange their first phase opium cessation licenses for the second phase. Most of those who have complied are in the majority, but there are some who are cunningly watching and refusing to exchange them. They should be arrested and dealt with strictly in accordance with the law. According to reports from various license-chasing agencies, many opium smokers have already paid the fees but have not yet collected their second phase new licenses. Now, they are limited to collecting them from the original license-chasing agency before the 15th of this month. Those who fail to do so will have their licenses cancelled and will not be allowed to collect them, and they will be treated as private opium smokers without a license. A notice was issued yesterday, and all opium smokers are required to comply.

In Nanjing, Mr. Ye Chucang, Mr. Chen Lifu, and other members of the Central Committee in Nanjing, as well as colleagues from the capital's press and friends of Mr. Hu, are preparing to hold a memorial service. Huaiyin: A Fire on Nanmen Street Kills Three People 81

In the small street inside the South Gate of this county, shops are lined up and the population is dense. Suddenly, at about 1 am on the night of the 3rd, a fire broke out in the Chen Yongtai Grocery Store, burning down as many as thirty or forty shops on the east and west sides of the street. Chen, the owner of the store, and two employees of other shops, Zhuang Yaoxian and others were burned to death. Most people say that the fire was caused by an employee of the Chen store holding a lamp to catch mosquitoes, which caused the bed curtain to catch fire. The employee saw the disaster he had caused and fled in the middle of the night. Li Yushu, the president of the Jishui Association here, has dispatched Tong Runtin and others to investigate the households one by one, preparing to distribute emergency relief.

Huaian: County Government Appeals for Relief Due to Water and Electrical Disaster 83

Since the great flood of 1931 caused disaster and displacement in the Eighth and Tenth Districts of this county, the vitality has not yet been restored. Suddenly, on May 11 of this year, strong winds, heavy rain, and hail fell, with the hail as large as a right block and as small as a chicken egg. Wheat ears and seedlings were almost completely destroyed, and many farmers' houses were damaged. The disaster area covered 16 townships and towns, and there were as many as 50,000 to 60,000 disaster victims. Not only is there no hope for the autumn harvest, and the people's food is worrying, but they are also eating in the wind and sleeping in the open, with nowhere to live. Old pain has not healed, and new disasters have struck again. Who is not suffering in such deep water? When the county government sent personnel to survey the area, they witnessed the disaster and felt heartbroken. The fields were full of hungry people, crying for food. In addition to temporarily accumulating and distributing seeds, other large amounts of money could not be planned to seek emergency relief. If they sit idly by at this time, not only will the disaster victims wait to die, but it is feared that it will affect public order. The county government has sent telegrams to the superiors, appealing for relief on their behalf, and has also sent telegrams to charitable organizations in Shanghai, soliciting donations separately. Once they are collected, they will be distributed immediately and a list will be created and announced.

Yangzhou: A Woman Selling Goods Drowns Near Zhentong Transport Boat 84

The Huaiyuan, a tugboat of the Dongchang Wheel of the Zhentong Company coming from Tai, arrived outside Yimen at about 3 pm on the 8th. Suddenly, Wang Bian, (33 years old) who was selling salted duck eggs on the boat, accidentally fell into the water when crossing from the wheel to the tugboat. The wheel continued to travel straight away. After the surrounding masses caught a glimpse of this, they furiously shouted for the boat to stop, to no avail, causing public outrage, the boat was hit by hurled tiles and stones, only then stopping. The nearby paddle boat found and retrieved the body. The Public Security Fifth Precinct detained the head of the boat Wu Guangui, and transferred him to the Public Security Bureau. When relatives of the deceased arrived upon hearing news, a search of her person revealed two dollars and three cents of silver, two dimes of silver, dozens of copper coins, a silver hairpin, a pair of golden bracelets. Her brother has been notified and is en route to attend to her affairs.

Gaoyou: All Districts Set Quotas for Leading Huai River Substitute Money 85

Starting this month, the collection of substitute money for guiding the Huai River in this county will be the responsibility of the newly appointed township chiefs, and the Bao chiefs will also bear joint responsibility. All businesses and households paying substitute money shall be based on the grain register and shall not be allowed to refuse or prevaricate. The amount of substitute money for each district shall be reallocated according to the approximate number of fields in each township and shall be determined for the four months of June, July, August, and September. It is estimated that the first district will pay 50,000 yuan, the second district 60,000 yuan, the third district 45,000 yuan, the fourth district 45,000 yuan, the fifth district 50,000 yuan, the sixth district 50,000 yuan, the seventh district 30,000 yuan, and the eighth district 40,000 yuan.

Jiashan: Conflict in Theater Results in Death 86

Since the end of last month, the Zhanghui Central Theater has invited a Shanghai theatrical troupe to perform, and the business has been very prosperous, with seats often full. Unexpectedly, yesterday, hundreds of workers from Taizhou broke into the theater without buying tickets. When they were stopped by the ticket seller, a conflict broke out, and both sides used weapons. Knives and scissors flew everywhere, and the order was completely disrupted. The women and children in the audience desperately tried to escape, scrambling over each other, and cries for help were heard everywhere. Five employees in the theater were seriously injured, one of whom was on the verge of death, lying in a pool of blood. He died the following afternoon. The local security corps' prior suppression was ineffective. After the incident, they arrested the perpetrators A Er and A Mao, but the rest escaped. The county's Public Security Bureau has now dispatched inspectors to investigate the matter in the countryside.

Xiaoshan, Merchant Driven to Suicide by Economic Oppression 87

In Xinlin Zhou, a village in the eastern part of this county, a merchant named Zhou Qingzhen, who used to run a business in Shanghai, was known to be quite wealthy. However, in the past two years, his business failed, and he owed others as much as two to three thousand taels of silver. A few days ago, two banks in Shanghai suspended operations, and Zhou had deposited three to four thousand yuan on behalf of others. Upon receiving news from Shanghai on the 7th, he immediately became mentally deranged. That evening, he hanged himself in his room and died. His family rushed to rescue him upon hearing the news, but he had already passed away. He left behind a wife and five children, making it difficult for the family to make a living.

Hangzhou, Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau Protects Passengers 88

Remnants of bandits under the command of Su and Liu have been harassing the Zhejiang border. After our security team, along with tax police and local militias, intercepted them, the bandits dispersed into smaller groups and fled in disarray. The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau, considering that the areas along the railway line, such as Jinhua, Changxi, and Longyou counties, although far from the bandits, are crucial to the safety of traveling passengers, has dispatched route protection teams to be stationed in various key locations for strict protection. Train schedules will remain normal.

Letter to the Editor 89

To the esteemed Editor of Your Esteemed Newspaper:

Regarding the news item published in your newspaper's Foreign Correspondence section on June 6th about the disappearance of the Director of Grain Collection in Haimen, after investigation, it has been determined that Cha Bingquan is not involved in any such situation. Furthermore, since assuming office, Mr. Cha has been diligent and selfless in his duties. It is believed that this is a misunderstanding based on rumors. The matter concerns reputation, and we fear it may mislead public opinion. Therefore, we are writing to request a correction.

Respectfully submitted,

Yuan Bingquan, Head of Tax Collection, Hai Dou County

To the Esteemed Editor of Shen Bao:

Regarding the news item in your newspaper on the 9th about the drowning of a young girl from a coal boat in Wuxi, the reported details are completely inconsistent with the facts. After the incident, the relatives of the deceased, Lü Fuhai and Song Youming, along with the assistant manager of our company, Li Guoliang, stated the true cause of death as falling into the river due to a broken punting pole. The court-appointed prosecutor also recorded this information, and all parties signed the document, which is on file with the broken pole for verification. There was no collision between two boats. Fearing confusion among the public, we hereby submit this letter requesting its publication in the "Letters to the Editor" column for clarification.

Respectfully submitted,

Xinji Steamboat Company

Ministry of Finance Allocates 20 Million in Certificates to Establish Relief Loan Committee for Industry and Commerce 90

Inviting Cai Zengji and 10 Others as Members, Implementing Loan According to Ministry's Principles After Establishment

Approved Issuance of 2.6 Million in Bonds to Qianye Industry, Minghua and Qing City Directors Seek Instructions from Kong

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, besides allocating 20 million in treasury certificates to relieve industry and commerce, the Ministry of Finance has also invited Cai Zengji and others as committee members. The committee will soon convene to manage the loans. The Qianye industry held a managers' meeting. The Ministry has ordered banks and Qianzhuang that have suspended operations to send personnel to supervise and investigate. The Minghua Bank shareholders' meeting did not meet the required quorum and was suspended. Qingdao City Government representatives met with Kong to seek instructions. Detailed information is as follows:

Inviting Committee Members to Manage Loans

Besides allocating 20 million in treasury certificates, to be held in custody by Cai Zengmou and others, as the second guarantee for loaning to industry and commerce according to the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry, the Ministry of Finance has also invited Cai Zengji (Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau), Wu Xingya (Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau), Du Yuesheng (Chairman of the Local Association), Wang Xiaolai (Speaker of the Municipal Council), Chen Guangfu (Chairman of the Banking Association), Wang Yansong (General Manager of the Xiaoye Bank), Qin Runqing (Chairman of the Qianye Association), Bei Songsun (Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China), Xi Demao (Manager of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank), Zhang Peishen (Manager of the Business Bureau of the Bank of Communications), and Yu Zuoting (Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce), a total of eleven people, as committee members.

Announcing Establishment of the Committee

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from the committee members yesterday that the letters of appointment from the Ministry of Finance have been received one after another yesterday. The first committee meeting will be held soon to announce the establishment of the Relief Loan Committee for Industry and Commerce. After the establishment, loans will be implemented according to the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry. The first guarantee will be the domestic goods manufactured by domestic goods factories and stores. The second guarantee will be the treasury certificates from the Ministry of Finance. As for mortgages and discounts, etc., the standards will be determined after the committee meeting. The address of the committee will likely be within the Central Bank.

Qianye Association Managers' Meeting

The Qianye Association held a managers' meeting at its headquarters on Ningbo Road at 10 AM the day before yesterday. Managers from 55 member Qianzhuang attended. Qin Runqing chaired the meeting and reported on the details of the Ministry of Finance's allocation of 25 million in 24th-year financial bonds to relieve the Qianye industry and the establishment of the Qianye Supervision Committee. Subsequently, discussions were held on the fundamental solutions to relieve the Qianye industry. The issue of "splitting heads and adding water" was also mentioned. The meeting adjourned around 11 AM. According to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, "splitting heads and adding water" refers to the interbank lending rates between banks and Qianzhuang. The daily rates soared to a peak of 70 cents, and even then, they were insufficient to meet demand.

Qianye Pledges 1.5 Million in Cash

After the Ministry of Finance allocated 25 million in bonds to relieve the Qianye industry and established a Supervision Committee to manage it, a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency inquired at the committee yesterday. Yesterday was Sunday, and the committee was closed as usual. By the deadline the night before last, the total amount of bonds issued to Qianzhuang that had applied to the committee with collateral and passed the review was 2.6 million in face value. Discounted at 60%, this amounted to 1.56 million in national currency, all of which were underwritten by the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Bank of Communications. Today, the committee will continue to review the collateral of various Qianzhuang at the Ningbo Road Qianye United Reserve.

Ministry Directive for Suspended Banks and Qianzhuang

The Ministry of Finance issued Directive No. 32, Shanghai Qianzi, stating: "Regarding the matter of issuing directives, this bank has declared a suspension of operations for liquidation. The savings deposits received should be fully liquidated and repaid within one month as ordered. Other debts should also be liquidated promptly and should not be deliberately delayed or opportunistically manipulated to the detriment of creditors' interests. Furthermore, prolonged delays should be avoided to prevent abuses and disputes, which would be contrary to the government's responsibility to protect people's property and maintain social credit. Therefore, the Ministry has specially stipulated six supervision and liquidation measures, set strict deadlines, and assigned personnel to supervise the liquidation. The aim is to ensure thorough liquidation and an early conclusion. In addition to assigning other supervision and liquidation personnel separately, this directive orders the bank to comply and not to disobey."

Minghua Shareholders' Meeting Yesterday Failed to Achieve Quorum

After Minghua Bank suspended operations, the shareholders' meeting was originally scheduled to be held at the Ningbo Association in Shanghai on Xizang Road at 2 PM yesterday. However, it failed to achieve the required quorum and was adjourned. The notice is recorded as follows: "Today, this bank convened an extraordinary shareholders' meeting. Only Yaoji and Chen Xifu, totaling 26 shares, came to the bank to collect admission tickets, which is less than the required quorum. According to regulations, the meeting cannot be held. Yesterday, we received Ministry of Finance Directive No. 32, Shanghai Qianzi (see above), and appointed Qiu Junzheng Lun as the supervision and liquidation officer. Therefore, we should wait quietly for the official supervision and liquidation. This is a notice." The bank's total shares are 27,500, and the shareholders who registered accounted for less than 1%.

Qingdao City Sends Representatives to Meet with Kong to Seek Instructions

According to lawyer Zhu Hongru, the custodian of the Minghua Bank documents, the extraordinary shareholders' meeting was adjourned due to the failure to meet the required quorum. It has now been decided to determine the next course of action after meeting with Qiu Zhenglun, the supervision and liquidation officer appointed by the Ministry of Finance. General Manager Zhang Jiongbo is still under the custody of the Qingdao Municipal Government. As for Guo Binghe, the Director of the Finance Bureau appointed by Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie, he has not yet been met. According to another source, Guo Binghe, Director of the Qingdao Finance Bureau, flew from Qingdao to Shanghai yesterday afternoon. His mission is to meet with Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi to seek instructions on the liquidation of Minghua Bank.

Domestic Goods Organizations Request to Participate

According to Guomen News Agency, the Shanghai Promoting Domestic Goods League Committee, based on the resolution of the 48th Standing Committee, has specially submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance requesting permission to send representatives to participate in the committee organized by the lending institutions so that domestic goods organizations can also understand the loan details.

International Labor Organization's China Branch Announces: Global Unemployment Exceeds 20 Million 94

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the International Labor Organization estimates that the global unemployment rate is approximately 25 million people, of which unemployed youth under the age of 25 account for a quarter, approximately 6 to 7 million people. The global unemployment statistics for January, February, and March of this year show better trends in most countries, but Belgium, France, Poland, and the Netherlands have increased compared to the same period last year. Bulgaria, Spain, and Yugoslavia have slightly increased. In March of this year, Denmark had 125,595 unemployed people, France had 544,567, Germany had 2,764,676, the United Kingdom had 2,285,463, Italy had 1,011,711, the Netherlands had 432,392, Sweden had 105,435, and the United States had 11,329,000 in January of this year.

ILO Discusses Relief: The current International Labor Conference, held in Geneva the day before yesterday, will specifically discuss this serious youth unemployment problem. Many countries have already taken various steps. The ILO believes that it is more appropriate to create recommendations than to formulate draft conventions for the youth unemployment problem. The ILO's relief plan focuses on creating technical schools and organizing vocational training centers within public employment agencies.

China's Unemployment Situation: Regarding the unemployment situation in China, according to the registration of the National Academic Work Advisory Office, from 1934 to March of this year, there were a total of 608 people. The number of people registered at the Shanghai Employment Agency from 1927 to 1934 was 19,260. Regarding the unemployment situation of graduates from public and private universities across the country, most schools do not have accurate statistics.

Citizens Purchase and Use Party and National Flags 97

Municipal Government Formulates Provisional Measures

In order to facilitate citizens' purchase and use of Party and national flags, the Shanghai Municipal Government has formulated eleven provisional measures for citizens' purchase and use of Party and national flags, which are hereby promulgated and implemented. Details are extracted as follows: (1) Each store and residence in this city shall purchase one Party flag and one national flag. (2) In cases where several families live in one residence, the landlord shall be responsible for providing the required Party and national flags. (3) On national holidays, Party and national flags shall be hung according to the prescribed format. Those who do not have a Party flag may only hang the national flag. Each Public Security Bureau and stores that manufacture and sell Party and national flags have "Flag Hanging Guidelines" available for consultation. (4) Those who do not have Party and national flags shall purchase them from designated or licensed stores that manufacture and sell Party and national flags before August of this year. The Party and national flags manufactured and sold by these stores shall comply with the provisions of Article 1 of the "Regulations on the Manufacture and Use of Party and National Flags" and shall be sold at the prescribed prices. (5) The Public Security Bureau shall urge each branch to investigate and report the exact number of stores and residences in the city that do not have Party and national flags before July. (6) The Municipal Government shall convene the flag merchants in the city to explain that the manufacture and sale of Party and national flags shall comply with the "Measures for the Management of Stores that Manufacture and Sell Party and National Flags" and shall apply to the Central Government for designation or licensing and shall register with the Public Security Bureau. (7) The Public Security Bureau and its branches shall conduct inspections at any time. If anyone fails to purchase Party and national flags or fails to hang Party and national flags on national holidays, the branch in charge shall summon and reprimand the offender for the first offense and report the homeowner's name to the Public Security Bureau. For repeat offenses, the branch shall report to the Public Security Bureau for punishment. (8) The Social Affairs Bureau shall inspect the Party and national flags manufactured and sold by each flag store at any time. If they do not conform to the prescribed format, they shall be corrected according to law. (9) The Municipal Government shall send personnel to inspect various locations in the city in stages. If it is found that any stores or residences do not comply with these measures, the branch in charge shall be punished for ineffective enforcement. (10) These measures may be revised at any time if there are any omissions. (11) These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

New Life Youth Service Corps Served and Advised at Tea Houses and Theaters Yesterday 101

Correcting Obscene Lyrics and Vulgar Tunes to Purify Morals, Instructing the Public to Abide by the New Life Movement Regulations

Yesterday, the athletes of the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association's Youth Service Corps provided service and advice at various tea houses and entertainment venues, corrected obscene lyrics and vulgar tunes, and instructed the public to abide by the regulations of the New Life Movement. Details are as follows:

Mobilizing the Entire Corps for Service

Yesterday was a regular weekend holiday. The Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association's Youth Service Corps mobilized the entire city, making use of the rest time of staff from various agencies and students from various schools, to provide service. They all wore armbands with the words "Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association Youth Service Corps, District X, Team X" in white letters on a blue background. Each team consisted of two to ten people, holding the New Life Regulations, and went to various tea houses and entertainment venues to provide service. The police advisory teams of each district branch advised the public along the way, maintaining strict order and refreshing the city's appearance.

Correcting Vulgar Tunes to Purify Morals

For the sake of attracting public attention, public entertainment venues inevitably present obscene lyrics and vulgar tunes. However, such obscene lyrics and vulgar tunes have a very profound and negative impact on social morality. Their corruption and decadence are beyond compare. The New Life Movement Promotion Association has previously established regulations to ban them. Yesterday, the New Youth Service Corps specifically inspected public places such as entertainment venues and book markets in Nanshi and Zhabei, and corrected those who performed obscene lyrics and vulgar tunes in order to purify morals.

Instructing the Public to Abide by Regulations

Yesterday was a regular weekend holiday, and the public flocked to various entertainment venues and tea houses. The New Life Service Corps, fearing that the public would be unrestrained in entertainment venues, baring their arms and legs and indulging their desires, which would be detrimental to public decency, distributed the New Life Regulations at any time and provided detailed instructions on aspects of compliance with the regulations, so that the public's actions, whether in family life, office hours, or entertainment, would conform to the New Life Movement requirements in order to achieve a subtle and transformative effect.

(7) According to the association's unified universal principle, personnel working in the district should receive appropriate training within the 24th year to achieve unified universalization. It was resolved to recommend Zheng Xigu, Yao Huiquan, and Feng Zanyuan to design methods and submit them to the council for discussion. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Good News for Visiting Huangshan 106

From Hangzhou to Huangshan in Just Nine Hours and Fifty-Two Minutes

Huangshan Mountain in Anhui Province is famous for its secluded scenery and magnificent wonders, especially the pine trees and rocks. Since the establishment of the Huangshan Construction Committee, it has been working hard on various construction projects with grand plans.
