Short Story

The Unfinished Painting 188

— Wu Yafei

In order to tidy up my bookshelf, I discovered a painting scroll in the corner of the cabinet. It was a "Willow Creek Angling" picture. But regrettably, it was only half finished, and my father had passed away before he could complete it! He has been gone for twenty years now, but since my mother gave me that unfinished painting, I have carefully kept it hidden in the bookshelf. I remember my mother saying to me with tears in her eyes at the time:

"Fei, this painting is your father's last possession and his only legacy. Because you were still young when he died and didn't understand anything, I'm giving you this painting now. You must carefully keep it as a memento of your father!" My mother cried as she spoke. Although I didn't know my father and don't remember his death, I do miss him very much.

I am now a father myself, and I can't help but feel somewhat afraid because my mother often told me that my father died very young, worn down by life. It makes me worry. Am I not young now? And the grindstone of life is already pressing down on my shoulders!

My father was originally a very lively and energetic young man, but later, due to life, burdens, and many unpleasant attacks, he became depressed and melancholy. And soon he contracted a lung disease. At that time, my mother and relatives comforted him like this:

"You should understand and not worry too much. Life still has to be lived, and your health is also important!" But he was very stubborn and didn't believe he would die.

"No, I cannot rest. For the sake of life, I must repay debts. I can't let the children go hungry, and debts cannot lose credibility. Can lung disease destroy my future and stop my struggle?" His tone was so firm, so courageous, not at all like a person with lung disease who was dying.

Life pressed tighter and tighter on him day by day, the debts never decreased, and the pressure on his shoulders grew heavier. So he began to doubt: "Has my future really been destroyed by lung disease? Can it really stop my final struggle? But life still has to go on! The debts still have to be repaid!" He doubted and dared not trust his own courage, and even grieved over the failure of his various struggles. "Alas! Has my ideal been completely shattered? Is there no hope at all?" Although he still didn't quite believe it, when he looked at the darkness around him, he felt that everything was empty.

Day after day, month after month, year after year, time flew quickly in his life. His lung disease gradually worsened with the passage of time, and his sorrow also increased with the lung disease. Every morning he had to cough up a lot of phlegm, often had night sweats and insomnia, his appetite was reduced by half, and his face was frighteningly pale. His cheekbones were high, his eyes were sunken, and if he lay on a wooden plank, people would surely suspect that he was no longer breathing.

Because there was no money, he was never treated. Although he took many folk remedies, they were like stones sinking into the sea, with no effect at all! My mother was very anxious, but what could she do? She could only watch helplessly as my father became weaker and weaker day by day. Finally, on a spring afternoon, he left us and left behind that final work he had created while ill – the unfinished painting – and departed!

Now, whenever I unfold this painting, I think of my deceased father, and at the same time, my tear ducts cannot help but erupt like a mountain flood!

"My father was worn down by life and died so young. I don't want to be like my father!" Now, whenever I think of these things, I tremble!

Talk

Peace and War 189

— Meng Ruo

Recently, a Belgian socialist leader, Mr. Vandervelde, gave a speech at a women's congress of the party, saying: "The world is currently at a crossroads, on the one hand, pursuing a policy of peace and disarmament, and on the other hand, continuing to engage in

Mr. Fan's words are very good. The world today is turbulent, hesitating at the crossroads of peace and war, presenting an extremely precarious and uneasy state. On the surface, all countries in the world seem to be deeply committed to peace. Their great powers are constantly running around and shouting out the tones of peace and disarmament. But in reality, everyone is fiercely competing in armaments under the mask of peace. A great misfortune for humanity is bound to come sooner or later.

However, although there are many ambitious politicians and military personnel in power in the world today who are frantically preparing for war, the general public truly loathes war and loves peace. As a practical example, recently the United Kingdom launched a peace voting movement, posing five questions and holding a public referendum. The results showed that the majority of the two million British people who participated in the vote were inclined towards peace. This is clear proof of the people's love of peace.

But the people's love of peace is useless, and world war is still unavoidable. The day before yesterday, two American journalists familiar with international affairs made a prediction about world war, saying that the world's military preparations are now too heavy, like a large powder keg that can be detonated even by a very fine fuse. This observation is now very accurate.

Therefore, although the world is still a world of peace, this world of peace cannot be maintained for long. As long as the countries are strong enough and the time is right, the second great massacre will begin. At that time, this world of peace will turn into a world of war.

Seaside 190

— Ai Tu

In the daytime, the scorching sun seems to burn everything on the seashore like fire, but everything on the seashore will never dry up. It is always oozing with yellow, gluey liquid, soaked by the sea water. However, often, the river that surrounds our garden often evaporates white light smoke like a red thread. Indeed, the water is about to reach the boiling point, and the fish raised in the river are also steamed to death, many floating on the surface, exuding a fishy and rancid smell, wave after wave swept into our souls with the sultry wind. Every summer, the southern seashore is like this. From morning to dusk, everything is burned by flames. Once, the weather was so terribly hot:

"It's going to rain, and this time it's going to be a big storm."

Sure enough, when the sun was setting in the west with flames, black clouds swung fearfully in the sky. Then came a rare, violent sea breeze, howling. After we finished our work, we cooked dinner in the thatched hut as usual, ate a large plate of green vegetables and some fish and shrimp, and drank plain soup cooked with salt water. At this moment, the black sky thundered terribly, crackling.

"I'm afraid we won't be able to sleep comfortably tonight. The storm has arrived."

As I spoke, Ah Hui and I began to patch up the gaps in the thatched hut. Because this thatched hut was also built by ourselves with old bricks and tiles and some palm leaves. It was very small and a bit like the dwellings of ancient hunters. Of course, it was not very strong, and it could not withstand the destruction of terrible storms. Moreover, experience told us that violent wind and rain would blow away the palm leaves on the roof of the thatched hut.

It was dark, and we were lying on the plank bed in the narrow thatched hut, trying to sleep. At this time, the wind became louder and more terrible, like a roaring tiger. The dog outside the door was barking, wagging its tail with a terrified look – at this time, the universe was desolate, especially on the desolate seashore, as if it were in the world of ghosts, and the surging waves were rolling endlessly. However, we were very tired, so what did we care about such a big storm? So, we fell asleep in the shaking of the thatched hut.

When our faces were wet with rain and we felt as cold as winter, we woke up in shock.

"Ah Hui, the palm leaves on the roof have been blown up by the wind. Fix it quickly."

So, we immediately lit the kerosene lamp, found a rope, and climbed onto the roof in the pouring rain with our shoulders bare. We repaired it for our lives, enduring the whippings of the wind and rain. At this time, the sky was all dark, thundering, and flashing lightning like long snakes. We were anxious, and our bodies felt terribly cold. After a long struggle, we finally repaired the thatched hut, but our bed was soaked.

It was another desolate nocturne, and we fell asleep tiredly. When the sun came out from the east with bright colors the next morning, we started living that same ordinary work again.

Night Talk 191

— Mansha

The distant long night covered her black veil from the starlight in the sky, and the nerves awakened from the exhaustion of the long day. Watching the empty tomb in the room, and when the lonely soul was tightly grasped by the lonely black hand, it suddenly sank into the lively memories of the past. What lively and interesting nights there were in the past!

It was the summer of the village, and the south wind brought the coolness of the South Sea. Under the melon trellis illuminated by the moon, how lively and interesting it was! My mother took a group of children, and the brothers and sisters were all immersed in touching stories. The mysterious night brought a mysterious atmosphere, and the actions of ghosts and foxes told in the stories frightened the small bodies to shrink and tremble. Now, the group of children have all become adults. The sisters have been married off, and the brothers are all running around for life. This night talk under the summer moon is no longer recoverable. I wanted to regain the fascinating power from the trembling stories, but this fantasy obviously cannot be reproduced. But at the same time, the good taste of this night talk sprouted from my heart and made me remember many times the taste of night talks.

On a certain shore of the South Sea, the sea tide slammed against the stone reef, roaring. The wind blew the huge tide advancing northward. Several of us young people were locked in a small building in a seaside hut, facing the small window for a long night of conversation. The flames of all life's topics burned from our deep hearts; we talked about the mysteries of life, the mysteries of philosophy, the beautiful qualities of literature and art, and other bold and unrestrained words. Youth swelled up with heat in our blood, and this heat spewed out light from everyone's mouth. The outer sea lake responded to our roar, and the sea breeze stirred up our desires. A sleepless night was buried in the edge of the conversation: the night continued to grow, and the conversation became sharper and sharper. Time was gradually consumed moment by moment? And the elegance and leisure of the night were dissolved in the blood of young people, and expressed from the froth of the mouth.

Time slipped to middle age, but was driven in the tropical night. Walking with friends in the coconut grove; love was attracted by the magnet of the equator, and a torrent of words slipped out of the corners of the mouth. The tall trees induced the mystery of the inner secretion of life, and the conversation between the two became as sweet as if they were fused together. We walked until midnight, and we forgot what we had said. A kind of hazy and lovely words kept pouring out of the corners of our mouths like a stream of water. We only felt it was lovely, felt it was sweetly strange and tasted good, but we didn't know what it was saying. These words were so close to us.

Thrown into the city of Shanghai by life, the sins of the world have been exposed in our hearts, and all the former hobbies have been changed completely. Often, we sighed at the impermanence of human affairs, the darkness of society, and our grief and depression. The vigorous conversation was completely consumed, but there was still a spark of rekindling for the future. Therefore, although the conversation was not sharp, it retained a dim color in the gray. All hopes, love, these big topics have been over in our conversations anyway, but the conversation of middle-aged people will deeply insert into the black veil of the night and consume the long night.

Now, not only has childhood become a thing of the past, but also the friends of youth are scattered east and west. All the objects of conversation have disappeared one by one before our eyes, and all the topics that provoke conversation are gradually dying. Life has become a lonely shadow in the black night before our eyes, and the soul is gradually becoming hollow. In front of my eyes, a small candlelight shines on my lonely shadow, and the black veil of the night is covering my heart. The object of the conversation has disappeared, and the night is swaying in the illusionary, frustrated, and lonely shadow. The memories of the beautiful conversation in the past envelop the soul even more lonely and gray, making people feel exceptionally disappointed.

Page 19

Pawn 192

— Qin Jian

(One of the Essays on Local Customs)

When I was a child, when adults took me to the street, I saw the only one or two pawnshops on the street. Facing the tall, large white walls with the terribly large "pawn" character, I had the same feeling as the "authentic medicinal materials" outside the pharmacy, the "official sauce" at the entrance of the sauce garden, and the "Namo Amitabha Buddha" on both sides of the temple - all around were terribly large black characters, who knew what they were doing inside? The difference was that the pawnshop was equipped with a counter that was higher than all the shops. For a child, it was simply a high wall! But what exactly was inside this high wall? No one knew clearly. Maybe it was mysterious and not something a child could know? But because of this, I felt a mystery about the large "pawn" character that made people's hats fall off when they looked at the top, and the counter that was more than twice as tall as my entire small body. I also felt an interest that was only suitable for reckoning in the heart of a child.

When I grew up a little and recognized two or three hundred characters, I eagerly followed the adults to the strange character that made people afraid, suspicious, but also made them feel interesting. So I also learned the crisp sound of "dang dang". But when I tried to explore the things inside this high counter, people just said that one sentence: "Children don't understand."

It's true that I didn't understand it. Every time I went to the street, I always sneaked a glance at the high counter, watching two or three people, empty-handed or carrying a package, with an indescribable look of embarrassment on their faces. Was it restraint and stagnation, or enthusiasm and worry? In short, those people, coming in and out, all had faces that didn't seem to be proud or happy. This was not wrong at all, but it was so incomprehensible and difficult to understand.

Now I have grown up completely. I have lost my childhood that will never return. I no longer have a child's heart, and no one will use the words "Children don't understand!" to spit and boast at me. When my torso grew from half the height of the high counter to the same height as the high counter, I fully understood the meaning of the strange large character, understood the tragedy inside this high counter, and lived as if I was rolling on a bed of nails. On days when some difficult encounters pushed people to the point of exhaustion, I also followed the others, standing in front of the high counter with a trembling and humble heart, and became an unfamiliar visitor in the shop marked with the large "pawn" character.

Living in a small city, so uncertain, empty and lonely, for lonely travelers in life, this strange and unpleasant "pawn" shop is just like a small inn in a desolate mountain. Seeing it on a desolate path at dusk, it may still be worth rejoicing (!); so, when there is a shortage of food for the family tomorrow, and acquaintances are so practical that they are preparing cold and crying expressions waiting for you, you can only remember the cold and frightening large character, and quietly pick out something, maybe take off the clothes you are wearing, maybe drop a small finger ring that is not worth much but is worn as a permanent souvenir. With an eager and humble mood, I hide and quietly stand under the high counter, waiting for the agreement of the pawnbroker and the payment of a little money. In this way, I tremblingly overcome another difficulty.

Now, I have learned the meaning of the word "pawn" from life, and it has turned from curiosity to fear for me, from comedy to tragedy. I would rather someone still say to me: "Children don't understand this kind of thing!"

However, I am no longer a child!

Pottery Kiln 193

— Ruizhi

In early summer in the South, the weather is already very hot. Early in the morning, the huge sun slipped out from behind the mountains in the east, and the earth was filled with heat. The breeze that blew across my face felt as if it was spewing out of a fire pit, scorching hot. The withered yellow rice seedlings in the fields, the dwarf trees on the hillsides, the chimneys on the farmhouses, all the scenery seemed lifeless without a trace of vitality. The pottery kilns spread out under the hillsides also seemed to be old and quietly lying in the morning sun. The road leading to the town, where there used to be a constant stream of people walking from morning to night, now doesn't even have the shadow of a stray dog.

Old Long, who had worked in the kiln firing porcelain since he was a child, was as thin as a beaten wild dog, his bones seemed to be exposed outside his skin, and his eyes were yellow and without a trace of light. Although he was only in his forties, his face was full of wrinkles, as if he were very old. At this time, he was walking in the fields, constantly looking at the sun in the sky, and then at the porcelain kiln without a trace of fire.

"It's been a full three months. If this goes on, there won't be any more bowls to be fired in the kiln. I've been eating this bowl of porcelain rice since I was a child, but I've never seen anything like this year when there hasn't been a fire for three months!" As he thought, his feet involuntarily walked towards the porcelain kiln. This was the way he was every day.

In the kiln that hadn't been fired for three months, there was a layer of clay everywhere, and the kiln holes were already covered with cobwebs. But the bowls pushed aside were stacked high, basket by basket. In the past, there had never been so many stored here. As soon as they were made, they were bought by the bowl dealers in the town, but now, they were like waste, piled up from three months ago to the present, and never moved. Old Long looked at the situation that he had seen countless times in the past three months, and his heart seemed to be numb without any emotion, just shaking his head and walking away quietly.

It was afternoon. On the road to the town, it was as lively as it used to be, with hundreds of men and women carrying hundreds of loads of bowls towards the town. Old Long and his son also each carried four loads of bowls, mixed in the crowd. But this image was clearly different from the past. In the past, it was this lively every day, and the road was never cut off from human traces. Although the people walking were all sweating and panting under the weight on their shoulders, they walked very energetically. The quarrels and laughter of women and men echoed everywhere. But today, although there were hundreds of people, they were all silent. There was no laughter at all, only low sighs and heavy breathing. Everyone's face was pale yellow. Each face, like a hungry dog, was terribly thin and dark. The pace of walking was so slow, and the sweat flowed across the dusty face, drawing black traces.

The river water was reddish, and the sun shone on it, making it even brighter. At this time, the cargo ships carrying bowls, which were parked on the shore, were lying in silence. The cabins were empty, without a basket of goods. This was just like the hundreds of people carrying bowls to the porcelain shops in the town. They were refused to buy by the shops. A group of people had no choice but to sit quietly by the river. They looked at the cargo ships that used to constantly transport goods out but were now empty, and their own hundreds of loads of unsold bowls. Hundreds of faces, hundreds of pairs of pale yellow eyes, just kept looking at each other.

Singing 194

Global Harmonica Association Regular Broadcast 195

Our country's harmonica expert Mr. Bao Mingshan has recently united with various famous harmonica players from within the country, including Yu Yu, Zhao Lianbi, Zheng Hongmo, and Zhang Qiguang, to form a Global Harmonica Research Association on the second floor of 503 North Sichuan Road. Since the Association announced in various newspapers last week that it was seeking members free of charge, the number of applicants has been very enthusiastic. There are still a few vacancies in each class. Those who aspire to learn and research harmonica music should not miss this opportunity. The members' study and research time has also been decided: the elementary class will meet every Saturday from 8:00 PM to 9:00 PM, and the research class will meet every Sunday from 8:00 PM to 9:00 PM. In order to enable members to practice and perform, the Association has decided to start next week and practice broadcasting on the Ye Mei Radio Station every Sunday from 11:30 AM to 12:00 PM.

Letter 196

To the esteemed editor,

Greetings. I recently read a letter in your newspaper on June 7th, stating that our society included Wang Tantantan and Wang Xiaodan in our program without their permission. This is not true. On the 29th of last month, the two ladies, along with Ms. Bao Xuexue and others, personally visited the Fuxing Radio Station to make guest appearances and expressed their desire to join our society. Due to the late hour, they did not fill out the application form, but both parties had agreed at the time. Therefore, our program should rightfully list them as singers for our society. However, Wang et al. did not come to the station to broadcast on the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd. Our society considered that the two had gone back on their word. Later, we learned that although Wang et al. liked to sing, they did not have the consent of their parents and could not fulfill their wishes to broadcast for our society. Therefore, our society, with understanding, did not question them. Who knew that Wang Jun Xiaolin would publish this news in your newspaper, which is extremely laughable. This matter concerns the reputation of our society, and we fear that the outside world will not understand the truth. Therefore, we hereby issue a solemn statement and ask you to publish it in a corner of your newspaper. We would be most grateful. Our society has already officially communicated with Wang Jun Xiaolin in a separate letter.

Respectfully,

Shanghai Starlight Society (Seal)

Movie News

Shanghai Anecdotes 197

The Shanghai Sound Film Company's substitute filming of "Little Aunt" has been completed, so the progress of "Peach Blossom Dream" is very rapid. Director Dan Duyu has not slept for several nights, but handles affairs as usual during the day. His spirit is truly amazing.

Miss Lei Mengna visited the Shanghai film studio and took several photos of the set of "Peach Blossom Dream." It is said that Lei may join "Peach Blossom Dream" to play a role.

Mr. Zhang Chong of Nanjing visited the Shanghai film studio and praised the interior scene of Peach Blossom Creek built for "Peach Blossom Dream" endlessly.

Gao Mangsheng has always been known as a fool, but his performance in "Peach Blossom Dream" is exceptionally profound and is the only promising talent in the film industry.

Second Performance of the Ant Troupe 198

Performing at the Lake Society on the 16th of this month

Since the Ant Troupe's first performance of "Jinbao" was a success, it has been actively preparing for its second performance. After months of effort, it has been officially scheduled to perform at the Beijing Road Lake Society on the 16th of this month. The troupe was founded by the famous cultural group Ant Society and has strong strength. In addition to the first show being offered free of charge to its more than 800 members, there will be two more shows at 2:00 PM and 8:00 PM in the afternoon. The scripts are "At Parting" by the British female poet "Mansfield" translated by Luo Jialun, President of Central University, "Chastity" by Japanese Kikuchi Kan, and "Two Friends in Distress" created by the troupe members themselves. All of them are works with profound meaning and moving plots. It is said that ticket sales have already begun, and major stores and bookstores on Nanjing Road and Simalu are selling them on consignment. It is expected that this performance by the troupe will once again cause a sensation.

The Release Period of "Hysteria" 199

The sound film "Hysteria" directed by Yueming, because it is a maiden work, and because everything has been newly planned, such as the sound studio, production equipment, and the additions and changes to the story, are all matters that consume a lot of energy and resources. Furthermore, because the initial setting of the "Hysteria" story is Sichuan, Ren Pengnian and his party also delayed for a considerable amount of time in Sichuan (of course, the filming of newsreels also took up a part of this time). It took several months to come back to shoot the interior scenes. From the beginning to the end, it took a full year. It can be seen that Yueming's own ability is not small, as she only shot one film in a year. Now, everything about "Hysteria" has been completed for a long time, so the reason for the delay in its release is actually because the films already scheduled by Jincheng are too crowded. Now this is a true and reliable message. After "Beginning of Man," it will be "Hysteria's" release period. Movie fans who have been waiting anxiously can find compensation in this amazing debut work.

"Goddess of Liberty" Discovers New Child Star Ren Ke 200

There is indeed a shortage of actors on the screen, and there is even a greater shortage of child roles. The child stars in "Goddess of Liberty" directed by Situ Huimin originally included Cai Weining and Cai Weixian, who are the two older ones. The play also needs a younger character to play the childish era of this children's drama character. After much searching, a brand new child star - Ren Ke - was discovered. He is only three years old, understands Mandarin and Shanghai dialect, can speak Cantonese, and can also act. Rather than saying that this is his innate inheritance, it is better to say that his acquired comprehension has helped his acting development. On the set, under the director's instructions, and with the praise of many viewers, he performed a variety of poses. Once, Shi Chao, who played his father, came back, and he knew to salute him and waved to him happily. But he doesn't understand that this is acting. The plot in the play has already achieved such reasonable results, it is no wonder that the actors from the Central Film Studio who came to Datong to visit praised him repeatedly.

Lianhua Express News 201

The Lianhua Northern Sound Machine is the latest invention. Its sound symbols are not wave-shaped, nor serrated, nor horizontal stripes. They are connected to each other little by little, looking like a string of candied haws.

The actors like to listen to Ma Xuweibang talk about the plot the most, because his speech has a well-modulated rhythm, allowing the listeners to have illusions in their eyes.

Lianhua actors Jin Yan and Shang Guanwu have recently been borrowed by other companies. Lao Jin stars in "Peach Blossom Fan" for Xinhua, and Lao Shang stars in "Hero of the Times" for Yihua.

Liu Jiqun has recently been seen carrying a cane, which is said to be the one given to him by his wife after she was cured of her disease.

Lianhua has discovered another newcomer, Huang Dai. This gentleman is currently working in the production department, but he will soon appear in several new films. It is expected that his villain style will achieve unprecedented success.

The songs in "Autumn Fan Lamp," "You Are My Lifeline," both the music and lyrics are from the hands of musicians and celebrities in the literary and art world, harmonious and beautiful, and unprecedented. After being released, they are recited by every household, as expected.
